\mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} pressure Generally this takes \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} form \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a1c0ce8c00e0b9ca5fe83f39420029640}{in}} this \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a306afc8f66ca909a765e72ad3a0c7840}{case}} we must allow material particles to be displaced transversely Since we have \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a3a84fbefe92af02054df0a78edc5afa4}{formulated}} our problem \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a1c0ce8c00e0b9ca5fe83f39420029640}{in}} terms \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} our formulation naturally produces a$<$ B $>$ plane strain$<$/B $>$ problem if we reduce \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} equations to two while \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a7316ec4bd7a423d6e7d3569960f6f1de}{remaining}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a1c0ce8c00e0b9ca5fe83f39420029640}{in}}-\/plane) displacements are only \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_ac80dee8a7753f546ac17d8bf504c8c78}{functions}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a1c0ce8c00e0b9ca5fe83f39420029640}{in}}-\/plane \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a064235c3a8f2dc8a4ba29a17e93660c2}{coordinates}}
\item 
when implementing such strain energy recall that any \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a70374e75c08d5fa9cc3a779fc7a6a32a}{invariants}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} metric \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a666ce285d52ee4f706072399558c7254}{tensors}} etc are \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} same as those \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} corresponding quantities$<$ HR $>$ subsection isotropic\+\_\+growth Isotropic growth Many biological tissues undergo growth processes For \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} cells that make up a solid tumour divide regularly and as a result \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} total mass \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} tumour increases If \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} growth occurs non uniformly so that certain parts \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} tumour grow faster than regions that grow more slowly restrain \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} expansion \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} their neighbours This process \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a7ba30fe6dbbf4fa4ea1e6c87e45036b8}{can}} induce significant growth stresses The scenario is \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_ad947b1bc5cb0f07d71f9bd4117e6bf25}{similar}} (but not identical) to that \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} thermal growth \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a1c0ce8c00e0b9ca5fe83f39420029640}{in}} which a non-\/uniform temperature distribution \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a1c0ce8c00e0b9ca5fe83f39420029640}{in}} a \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a2f87118efdcc85452e8d61dead34f6ae}{body}} creates thermal stresses.(The important difference between these two \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_ae0d6c69b58bd7605b13f112f938c0c2c}{cases}} is that \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a1c0ce8c00e0b9ca5fe83f39420029640}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} latter process mass is conserved -\/-\/ thermal expansion only leads to an increase \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a1c0ce8c00e0b9ca5fe83f39420029640}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} volume occupied by \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} material

\mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} their neighbours This process \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a7ba30fe6dbbf4fa4ea1e6c87e45036b8}{can}} induce significant growth stresses The scenario is whereas biological growth via cell division increases \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} mass \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aa05577448c7fd76410512f799a15ca6e}{the}} tumour It is easy to incorporate such growth {\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_a863027693ad1a74ca432dc45f0d56ec5}{delta}} E \mbox{[}incompressibility\mbox{]} \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_aea73b66df2d8d353363b5b18e1122d13}{f}} which ensures that the volume \mbox{\hyperlink{solid__theory_8txt_af867b058ca0bd3b0e7e20fa32e3fdfb6}{of}} infinitesimal
